module: srl_nokia-acl
  +--rw acl
     +--rw ipv4-filter* [name]
     |  +--rw name                     srl_nokia-comm:name
     |  +--rw description?             srl_nokia-comm:description
     |  +--rw subinterface-specific?   enumeration
     |  +--rw statistics-per-entry?    boolean
     |  +--ro last-clear?              srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |  +--ro statistics
     |  +--rw entry* [sequence-id]
     |     +--rw sequence-id     uint32
     |     +--rw description?    srl_nokia-comm:description
     |     +--ro tcam-entries
     |     |  +--ro linecard* [slot]
     |     |     +--ro slot               uint8
     |     |     +--ro single-instance?   uint16
     |     |     +--ro input-total?       uint16
     |     |     +--ro output-total?      uint16
     |     +--rw action
     |     |  +--rw (action)?
     |     |     +--:(accept)
     |     |     |  +--rw accept!
     |     |     |     +--rw log?   boolean {srl_nokia-feat:jericho2}?
     |     |     +--:(drop)
     |     |        +--rw drop!
     |     |           +--rw log?   boolean
     |     +--rw match
     |     |  +--rw destination-ip
     |     |  |  +--rw prefix?    srl_nokia-comm:ipv4-prefix
     |     |  |  +--rw address?   srl_nokia-comm:ipv4-address
     |     |  |  +--rw mask?      srl_nokia-comm:ipv4-address
     |     |  +--rw fragment?           boolean
     |     |  +--rw first-fragment?     boolean
     |     |  +--rw icmp
     |     |  |  +--rw type?   srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:icmp-type
     |     |  |  +--rw code*   uint8
     |     |  +--rw protocol?           srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:ip-protocol-type
     |     |  +--rw source-ip
     |     |  |  +--rw prefix?    srl_nokia-comm:ipv4-prefix
     |     |  |  +--rw address?   srl_nokia-comm:ipv4-address
     |     |  |  +--rw mask?      srl_nokia-comm:ipv4-address
     |     |  +--rw destination-port
     |     |  |  +--rw operator?   srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:operator
     |     |  |  +--rw value?      srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type
     |     |  |  +--rw range
     |     |  |     +--rw start?   srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type
     |     |  |     +--rw end?     srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type
     |     |  +--rw source-port
     |     |  |  +--rw operator?   srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:operator
     |     |  |  +--rw value?      srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type
     |     |  |  +--rw range
     |     |  |     +--rw start?   srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type
     |     |  |     +--rw end?     srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type
     |     |  +--rw tcp-flags?          string
     |     +--ro statistics
     |        +--ro last-clear?      srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |        +--ro aggregate
     |        |  +--ro in-matched-packets?    srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |        |  +--ro in-last-match?         srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |        |  +--ro out-matched-packets?   srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |        |  +--ro out-last-match?        srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |        +--ro per-interface
     |           +--ro subinterface* [name]
     |              +--ro name                   string
     |              +--ro in-matched-packets?    srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |              +--ro in-last-match?         srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |              +--ro out-matched-packets?   srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |              +--ro out-last-match?        srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |              +--ro last-clear?            srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     +--rw ipv6-filter* [name]
     |  +--rw name                     srl_nokia-comm:name
     |  +--rw description?             srl_nokia-comm:description
     |  +--rw subinterface-specific?   enumeration
     |  +--rw statistics-per-entry?    boolean
     |  +--ro last-clear?              srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |  +--ro statistics
     |  +--rw entry* [sequence-id]
     |     +--rw sequence-id     uint32
     |     +--rw description?    srl_nokia-comm:description
     |     +--ro tcam-entries
     |     |  +--ro linecard* [slot]
     |     |     +--ro slot               uint8
     |     |     +--ro single-instance?   uint16
     |     |     +--ro input-total?       uint16
     |     |     +--ro output-total?      uint16
     |     +--rw action
     |     |  +--rw (action)?
     |     |     +--:(accept)
     |     |     |  +--rw accept!
     |     |     |     +--rw log?   boolean {srl_nokia-feat:jericho2}?
     |     |     +--:(drop)
     |     |        +--rw drop!
     |     |           +--rw log?   boolean
     |     +--rw match
     |     |  +--rw destination-ip
     |     |  |  +--rw prefix?    srl_nokia-comm:ipv6-prefix
     |     |  |  +--rw address?   srl_nokia-comm:ipv6-address
     |     |  |  +--rw mask?      srl_nokia-comm:ipv6-address
     |     |  +--rw icmp6
     |     |  |  +--rw type?   srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:icmp6-type
     |     |  |  +--rw code*   uint8
     |     |  +--rw next-header?        srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:ip-protocol-type
     |     |  +--rw source-ip
     |     |  |  +--rw prefix?    srl_nokia-comm:ipv6-prefix
     |     |  |  +--rw address?   srl_nokia-comm:ipv6-address
     |     |  |  +--rw mask?      srl_nokia-comm:ipv6-address
     |     |  +--rw destination-port
     |     |  |  +--rw operator?   srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:operator
     |     |  |  +--rw value?      srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type
     |     |  |  +--rw range
     |     |  |     +--rw start?   srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type
     |     |  |     +--rw end?     srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type
     |     |  +--rw source-port
     |     |  |  +--rw operator?   srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:operator
     |     |  |  +--rw value?      srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type
     |     |  |  +--rw range
     |     |  |     +--rw start?   srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type
     |     |  |     +--rw end?     srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type
     |     |  +--rw tcp-flags?          string
     |     +--ro statistics
     |        +--ro last-clear?      srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |        +--ro aggregate
     |        |  +--ro in-matched-packets?    srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |        |  +--ro in-last-match?         srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |        |  +--ro out-matched-packets?   srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |        |  +--ro out-last-match?        srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |        +--ro per-interface
     |           +--ro subinterface* [name]
     |              +--ro name                   string
     |              +--ro in-matched-packets?    srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |              +--ro in-last-match?         srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |              +--ro out-matched-packets?   srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |              +--ro out-last-match?        srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |              +--ro last-clear?            srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     +--rw cpm-filter
     |  +--rw ipv4-filter
     |  |  +--rw statistics-per-entry?   boolean
     |  |  +--ro last-clear?             srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |  |  +--rw entry* [sequence-id]
     |  |     +--rw sequence-id     uint32
     |  |     +--rw description?    srl_nokia-comm:description
     |  |     +--ro tcam-entries?   uint16
     |  |     +--rw action
     |  |     |  +--rw (action)?
     |  |     |     +--:(accept)
     |  |     |     |  +--rw accept!
     |  |     |     |     +--rw log?          boolean {srl_nokia-feat:jericho2}?
     |  |     |     |     +--rw rate-limit
     |  |     |     |        +--rw system-cpu-policer?    -> ../../../../../../../policers/system-cpu-policer/name
     |  |     |     |        +--rw distributed-policer?   -> ../../../../../../../policers/policer/name {srl_nokia-feat:trident3 or srl_nokia-feat:jericho2}?
     |  |     |     +--:(drop)
     |  |     |        +--rw drop!
     |  |     |           +--rw log?   boolean
     |  |     +--rw match
     |  |     |  +--rw destination-ip
     |  |     |  |  +--rw prefix?    srl_nokia-comm:ipv4-prefix
     |  |     |  |  +--rw address?   srl_nokia-comm:ipv4-address
     |  |     |  |  +--rw mask?      srl_nokia-comm:ipv4-address
     |  |     |  +--rw fragment?           boolean
     |  |     |  +--rw first-fragment?     boolean
     |  |     |  +--rw icmp
     |  |     |  |  +--rw type?   srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:icmp-type

     |  |     |  |  +--rw address?   srl_nokia-comm:ipv4-address
     |  |     |  |  +--rw mask?      srl_nokia-comm:ipv4-address
     |  |     |  +--rw destination-port
     |  |     |  |  +--rw operator?   srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:operator
     |  |     |  |  +--rw value?      srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type
     |  |     |  |  +--rw range
     |  |     |  |     +--rw start?   srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type
     |  |     |  |     +--rw end?     srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type
     |  |     |  +--rw source-port
     |  |     |  |  +--rw operator?   srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:operator
     |  |     |  |  +--rw value?      srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type
     |  |     |  |  +--rw range
     |  |     |  |     +--rw start?   srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type
     |  |     |  |     +--rw end?     srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type
     |  |     |  +--rw tcp-flags?          string
     |  |     +--ro statistics
     |  |        +--ro matched-packets?       srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |  |        +--ro last-match?            srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |  |        +--ro last-clear?            srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |  |        +--ro distributed-policer {srl_nokia-feat:trident3 or srl_nokia-feat:jericho2}?
     |  |        |  +--ro conforming-packets?   srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |  |        |  +--ro conforming-octets?    srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |  |        |  +--ro exceeding-packets?    srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |  |        |  +--ro exceeding-octets?     srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |  |        +--ro system-cpu-policer
     |  |           +--ro conforming-packets?   srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |  |           +--ro conforming-octets?    srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |  |           +--ro exceeding-packets?    srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |  |           +--ro exceeding-octets?     srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |  +--rw ipv6-filter
     |     +--rw statistics-per-entry?   boolean
     |     +--ro last-clear?             srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta

     |        +--rw description?    srl_nokia-comm:description
     |        +--ro tcam-entries?   uint16

     |        |     +--:(accept)

     |        |  |  +--rw value?      srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type

     |           |  +--ro exceeding-octets?     srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64

     |              +--ro exceeding-packets?    srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64

     |  +--rw ipv4-filter

     |  |     +--rw sequence-id     uint32

     |  |     |     +--:(accept)

     |  |     |        +--rw copy!
     |  |     +--rw match
     |  |        +--rw destination-ip
     |  |        |  +--rw prefix?    srl_nokia-comm:ipv4-prefix
     |  |        |  +--rw address?   srl_nokia-comm:ipv4-address
     |  |        |  +--rw mask?      srl_nokia-comm:ipv4-address

     +--rw policers
     |  +--rw system-cpu-policer* [name]
     |  |  +--rw name                srl_nokia-comm:name
     |  |  +--rw entry-specific?     boolean
     |  |  +--rw peak-packet-rate?   uint32
     |  |  +--rw max-packet-burst?   uint32
     |  |  +--ro statistics
     |  |     +--ro conforming-packets?   srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |  |     +--ro conforming-octets?    srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |  |     +--ro exceeding-packets?    srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |  |     +--ro exceeding-octets?     srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |  |     +--ro last-clear?           srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |  +--rw policer* [name] {srl_nokia-feat:trident3 or srl_nokia-feat:jericho2}?
     |     +--rw name              srl_nokia-comm:name
     |     +--rw entry-specific?   boolean
     |     +--rw peak-rate?        uint32
     |     +--rw max-burst?        uint32
     |     +--ro statistics
     |        +--ro conforming-packets?   srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |        +--ro conforming-octets?    srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |        +--ro exceeding-packets?    srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |        +--ro exceeding-octets?     srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |        +--ro last-clear?           srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     +--rw system-filter {srl_nokia-feat:trident3}?

     |  |     |  |  +--rw code*   uint8
     |  |     |  +--rw protocol?           srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:ip-protocol-type
     |  |     |  +--rw source-ip
     |  |     |  |  +--rw prefix?    srl_nokia-comm:ipv4-prefix
     |  |     |  |  +--rw address?   srl_nokia-comm:ipv4-address
     |  |     |  |  +--rw mask?      srl_nokia-comm:ipv4-address
     |  |     |  +--rw destination-port
     |  |     |  |  +--rw operator?   srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:operator
     |  |     |  |  +--rw value?      srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type
     |  |     |  |  +--rw range
     |  |     |  |     +--rw start?   srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type
     |  |     |  |     +--rw end?     srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type
     |  |     |  +--rw source-port
     |  |     |  |  +--rw operator?   srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:operator
     |  |     |  |  +--rw value?      srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type
     |  |     |  |  +--rw range
     |  |     |  |     +--rw start?   srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type
     |  |     |  |     +--rw end?     srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type
     |  |     |  +--rw tcp-flags?          string
     |  |     +--ro statistics
     |  |        +--ro matched-packets?   srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
     |  |        +--ro last-match?        srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |  |        +--ro last-clear?        srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |  +--rw ipv6-filter
     |     +--ro last-clear?   srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta
     |     +--rw entry* [sequence-id]
     |        +--rw sequence-id     uint32
     |        +--rw description?    srl_nokia-comm:description
     |        +--ro tcam-entries?   uint16
     |        +--rw action
     |        |  +--rw (action)?
     |        |     +--:(accept)
     |        |     |  +--rw accept!
     |        |     +--:(drop)
     |        |        +--rw drop!
     |        |           +--rw log?   boolean
     |        +--rw match
     |        |  +--rw destination-ip
     |        |  |  +--rw prefix?    srl_nokia-comm:ipv6-prefix
     |        |  |  +--rw address?   srl_nokia-comm:ipv6-address
     |        |  |  +--rw mask?      srl_nokia-comm:ipv6-address
     |        |  +--rw icmp6
     |        |  |  +--rw type?   srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:icmp6-type
     |        |  |  +--rw code*   uint8
     |        |  +--rw next-header?        srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:ip-protocol-type
     |        |  +--rw source-ip
     |        |  |  +--rw prefix?    srl_nokia-comm:ipv6-prefix
     |        |  |  +--rw address?   srl_nokia-comm:ipv6-address
     |        |  |  +--rw mask?      srl_nokia-comm:ipv6-address
     |        |  +--rw destination-port
     |        |  |  +--rw operator?   srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:operator
     |        |  |  +--rw value?      srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type
     |        |  |  +--rw range
     |        |  |     +--rw start?   srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type
     |        |  |     +--rw end?     srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type
     |        |  +--rw source-port
     |        |  |  +--rw operator?   srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:operator
     |        |  |  +--rw value?      srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type
     |        |  |  +--rw range
     |        |  |     +--rw start?   srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type
     |        |  |     +--rw end?     srl_nokia-pkt-match-types:l4-port-type
     |        |  +--rw tcp-flags?          string
     |        +--ro statistics
     |           +--ro matched-packets?   srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64

           +--rw srl_nokia-micro-bfd:required-minimum-receive?            uint32
           +--rw srl_nokia-micro-bfd:detection-multiplier?                uint8
           +--ro srl_nokia-micro-bfd:member-interface* [name]
              +--ro srl_nokia-micro-bfd:name                                string
              +--ro srl_nokia-micro-bfd:session-state?                      bfd-session-state

              +--ro srl_nokia-micro-bfd:last-failure-time?                  srl_nokia-comm:date-and-time-delta

              +--ro srl_nokia-micro-bfd:remote-diagnostic-code?             bfd-diagnostic-code
              +--ro srl_nokia-micro-bfd:remote-minimum-receive-interval?    uint32
              +--ro srl_nokia-micro-bfd:remote-control-plane-independent?   boolean
              +--ro srl_nokia-micro-bfd:active-transmit-interval?           uint32
              +--ro srl_nokia-micro-bfd:active-receive-interval?            uint32
              +--ro srl_nokia-micro-bfd:remote-multiplier?                  uint8
              +--ro srl_nokia-micro-bfd:async!

        +--ro srl_nokia-vxlan-tunnel:statistics {srl_nokia-feat:platform-7220-d2 or srl_nokia-feat:platform-7220-d3}?
           +--ro srl_nokia-vxlan-tunnel:in-octets?              srl_nokia-comm:zero-based-counter64
